&webhookutil.ErrCallingWebhook{WebhookName: h.Name, Reason: fmt.Errorf(\"failed to call webhook: %w\", err), Status: status}\n311: \t}\n312: \tspan.AddEvent(\"Request completed\")\n313: \n314: \tresult, err := webhookrequest.VerifyAdmissionResponse(uid, true, response)\n315: \tif err != nil {\n316: \t\treturn false, &webhookutil.ErrCallingWebhook{WebhookName: h.Name, Reason: {\n334: \t\treturn false, nil\n335: \t}\n336: \tpatchObj, err := jsonpatch.DecodePatch(result.Patch)\n337: \tif err != nil {\n338: \t\treturn false, &webhookutil.ErrCallingWebhook{WebhookName: h.Name, Reason: fmt.Errorf(\"received undecodable patch in webhook response: %w\", err), Status: apierrors.NewServiceUnavailable(\"error decoding patch in webhook response\")}\n339: \t}\n340: \n341: \tif len(patchObj) == 0 {\n342: \t\treturn false, nil\n343: \t}\n344: \n345: \t// if a non-empty patch was provided, and we have no object we can apply it to (e.g. a DELETE admission operation), error\n346: \tif attr.VersionedObject == nil {\n347: \t\treturn false, apierrors.NewInternalError(fmt.Errorf(\"admission webhook %q attempted to modify the object, which is not supported for this Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → callAttrMutatingHook() → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) → callHook() (parallel) → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → callAttrMutatingHook() → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) → callHook() (parallel) → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n   214→}\n   215→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of three main phases:\\n\\n## 1. Webhook Admission Controller Entry Points\\n\\nTwo admission plugins serve as the entry points:\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Plugin struct implementing admission.MutationInterface, with Admit() method that delegates to Webhook.Dispatch()\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Plugin struct implementing admission.ValidationInterface, with Validate() method that delegates to Webhook.Dispatch()\\n\\n## 2. Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → callAttrMutatingHook() → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) → callHook() (parallel) → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n}\n","numLines":215,"startLine":1,"totalLines":215}}}

Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → callAttrMutatingHook() → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) → callHook() (parallel) → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":210,"oldLines":5,"newStart":210,"newLines":5,"lines":["       \"symbol\": \"Dispatch\"","     }","   ],","-  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of three main phases:\\n\\n## 1. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → callAttrMutatingHook() → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() → Dispatch() → ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) → callHook() (parallel) → REST client → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"","+  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of the following key components:\\n\\n## 0.
